	@Test  
    public void executSessionOne() throws InterruptedException
	{
	    System.setProperty("webdriver.chrome.driver", "C:\\temp\\java\\java\\chromedriver.exe");	
        WebDriver driver = new ChromeDriver(); 
        driver.get("http://192.168.1.60/finrest/");
        driver.manage().window().maximize();
          driver.manage().timeouts().implicitlyWait(60, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
        driver.findElement(By.id("uc_login_txtusername")).sendKeys("admin");
        driver.findElement(By.id("uc_login_txtpassword")).sendKeys("KRC@ADMIN");
        driver.findElement(By.id("uc_login_btnlogin")).click();
 	 driver.findElement(By.id("menu1")).click();;
	   driver.findElement(By.id("uc_menu_td_sub_menu1")).click();; 
	  //Select Gender.
	    Select dropdown = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("ddlsal")));
	    dropdown.selectByValue("Mr.");
	     //Enter Name, Middle Name, Last Name
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtfname")).sendKeys("Chetan");;
	   driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtmname")).sendKeys("Ganesh");
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtlname")).sendKeys("Chougala");
	    //Select Constitution.
	    Select Constitution = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_ddlconstitution")));
	    Constitution.selectByValue("Individual");
	    //Select Occupation.
	    Select Occupation = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("ddloccuption")));
	    Occupation.selectByValue("Salaried"); 
	    //Enter Date.
	   driver.findElement(By.id("txtdobdate")).sendKeys("11/25/1991");
	 // date.sendKeys(Keys.TAB);
		    //Enter Caste.
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcaste")).sendKeys("Hindu");
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcaste")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcaste")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcaste")).sendKeys(Keys.TAB); 
	    //Enter Address.
	  driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtcadd")).sendKeys("Acharya Galli, Shahpur");    
	  //Select State.
	    driver.findElement(By.id("ddlcstate")).sendKeys("Karnataka");
	 Thread.sleep(25000);
		   driver.findElement(By.id("ddlcdistrict")).sendKeys("Belagavi");     
	Thread.sleep(20000);
     driver.findElement(By.id("ddlccity")).sendKeys("Belagavi");
	         //driver.findElement(By.id("ddlccity")).sendKeys(Keys.TAB);
 Thread.sleep(24000);
	//Enter Area.
	    WebElement Area = driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea"));
	    //driver.manage().timeouts().implicitlyWait(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
	    Area.sendKeys("Majgav"); 
	      driver.manage().timeouts().implicitlyWait(60, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea")).sendKeys(Keys.TAB);
	  //Enter landmark.
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtclandmark")).sendKeys("Near temple");	     
	  //Enter Pincode.
	  driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtcpin")).sendKeys("590001");
		    //Select Permanent Address.
	    driver.findElement(By.id("chkcopy")).click();
	 Thread.sleep(25000);
	 // Enter Pan
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtpan")).sendKeys("ASDFG1200H");;
	 // Enter Adhar
	driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtuid")).sendKeys("123456789100");	     
	 // Enter Mobile Number.
	  driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtmno")).sendKeys("9448191400");
	 // Enter email.
	   driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtemail")).sendKeys("chetan@gmail.com");	
	  //Select Customer Type.
	    Select cust = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_ddlmtype")));
	    cust.selectByValue("Member");   
	  //Select Martial Status.
	    Select Mar = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_ddlMaritalStatus")));
	    Mar.selectByValue("Single");	    
	  //Enter Introducer.
	   driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtintrunm")).sendKeys("Ajit"); 
	    //Introducer.click();
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtintrunm")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN); 
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtintrunm")).sendKeys(Keys.ENTER); 
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='fileIdProof']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\images\\id.jpg");
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='fileAddProof']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\address.jpg");
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='filephoto']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\photo.jpg");
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='filesign']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\signature.jpg");
		  WebElement element = driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='BodyContent_ctl00_btnSave']"));
	    ((JavascriptExecutor) driver).executeScript("arguments[0].scrollIntoView(true);", element); 
	    Thread.sleep(4000);
	   driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='BodyContent_ctl00_btnSave']")).click();
}

	 Thread.sleep(25000);
		   driver.findElement(By.id("ddlcdistrict")).sendKeys("Belagavi");     
	Thread.sleep(20000);
     driver.findElement(By.id("ddlccity")).sendKeys("Belagavi");
	         //driver.findElement(By.id("ddlccity")).sendKeys(Keys.TAB);
 Thread.sleep(24000);
	//Enter Area.
	    WebElement Area = driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea"));
	    //driver.manage().timeouts().implicitlyWait(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
	    Area.sendKeys("Majgav"); 
	      driver.manage().timeouts().implicitlyWait(60, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN);
	    driver.findElement(By.id("txtcarea")).sendKeys(Keys.TAB);
	  //Enter landmark.
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtclandmark")).sendKeys("Near temple");	     
	  //Enter Pincode.
	  driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtcpin")).sendKeys("590001");
		    //Select Permanent Address.
	    driver.findElement(By.id("chkcopy")).click();
	 Thread.sleep(25000);

	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtpan")).sendKeys("ASDFG1216H");;

	driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtuid")).sendKeys("123456789127");

	  driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtmno")).sendKeys("9448191418");
	 // Enter email.
	   driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtemail")).sendKeys("chetan@gmail.com");	
	  //Select Customer Type.
	    Select cust = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_ddlmtype")));
	    cust.selectByValue("Member");   
	  //Select Martial Status.
	    Select Mar = new Select(driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_ddlMaritalStatus")));
	    Mar.selectByValue("Single");	    
	  //Enter Introducer.
	   driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtintrunm")).sendKeys("Ajit"); 
	    //Introducer.click();
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtintrunm")).sendKeys(Keys.DOWN); 
	    driver.findElement(By.id("BodyContent_ctl00_txtintrunm")).sendKeys(Keys.ENTER); 
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='fileIdProof']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\images\\id.jpg");
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='fileAddProof']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\address.jpg");
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='filephoto']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\photo.jpg");
	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='filesign']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\signature.jpg");
		  WebElement element = driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='BodyContent_ctl00_btnSave']"));
	    ((JavascriptExecutor) driver).executeScript("arguments[0].scrollIntoView(true);", element); 
	    Thread.sleep(4000);
	   driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='BodyContent_ctl00_btnSave']")).click();
}

	   driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='BodyContent_ctl00_btnSave']")).click();
}

	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='fileIdProof']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\images\\id.jpg");

	    driver.findElement(By.xpath(".//*[@id='filephoto']")).sendKeys("C:\\temp\\java\\Images\\photo.jpg");
